name:Êàë‚ÄçÂè´‚ÄçËéé‚ÄçËéé
info:Deluxe Room King
info:Stayed in October 2022
info:Other
info:4 Reviews
rating:4
posted:Posted October 12, 2022
msg:This is an honest review that is not meant to dissuade anyone but to offer a thorough unbiased review. My opinion of New World before my stay was that it was a 5 star hotel, it certainly wasn't horrible, but after my stay and comparing to other Dalian hotels in its league that I've stayed in, think it doesn't fit the bill for a 5 star hotel. I can't complain about the service, Check in was swift and we got a free room upgrade and spa coupons, but the hotel room carpet was stained, there was dust in some places and the furniture and room amenities are aging, slightly dated and need to be improved (I didn't feel the need to zoom in on those issues so the pictures wont reflect this) . I loved that there were lovely art pieces throughtout the hotel and the fitness centre was top notch especially the heated pool. The breakfast buffet had fewer options than expected for a hotel of that standard but it was honestly delicious and satisfactory, they had both Chinese and Western dishes, fruit and cereal. The waitresses from Guo restaurant had the best service they went out of their way to make our dinner pleasant. The most disconcerting issue I had with New World was that the room deposit refund took longer than I've ever experienced, I found it highly unusual and somewhat disappointing because I've stayed in a lot of 5 star hotels and usually the refund is instant but they told us it would take up to 3 days. Maybe this is standard practice for them but it made no sense to me and I've never had to wait that long. In any case surely it doesn't take 3 days to check a room!

msg:The hotel is in an excellent location, very close to Zhongshan Square, the center of Dalian City, and not far away is Donggang, so the hotel room can see both the bustling street scene and some sea view. PS: Maybe I live in a coastal city and am not so interested in a full sea view hotel. The local downtown street view + sea view room is more in line with my expectations.
My friend and I are both swimming enthusiasts. The hotel has a swimming pool, and a high-value swimming pool makes the experience much more upgraded. I swam once on the night of check-in and again at noon the next day. The swimming pool is beautiful during sunny days. From the effect of light and shadow, the designer is very attentive (unfortunately, neither of us brought a mobile phone)
The hotel breakfast is also great. It is open until 10:30 on weekends and eaten directly as brunch. Beef rice noodles are recommended.
After breakfast, take a walk to the Harbor Square. You can see some historical buildings along the way. The streets are full of French plane trees. This season is neither cold nor hot, which is very suitable for citywalk.
By the way, I will advertise the Yunnan mushroom rice noodles and Hongda barbecue around the hotel. They are delicious and not expensive.
In short, I will choose to stay in New World next time I come to Dalian.

msg:Traveling in Dalian, I stayed at the New World Hotel, which is on the must-stay list, and I was always satisfied. This time, the main reason was that I wanted to check in at Gangdong 5th Road, and it was convenient to go to the New World Hotel on Renmin Road in the city center. There were delicious food and fun things to do around it within three or four kilometers by taxi!

A handsome manager named Sun at the front desk provided great service and helped me upgrade to the Juxianhui Executive Room. The room was really nice and on the same floor as the Executive Lounge. Breakfast, afternoon tea, and happy hour were all convenient!

Of course, the buffet restaurant on the first floor has a richer variety! There are both Chinese and Western styles, and the seafood porridge is good, and it has been updated for two consecutive days. The rooms at Juxianhui are very good value. In addition to having a higher view, the drinks in the mini bar are free, the dishes during happy hour taste great, and there are conference rooms that can be used for free.

Recently, the buffet dinner at this hotel has been very popular in Dalian! You can eat all kinds of seafood, Japanese sashimi, small hot pot, and tomahawk steak for more than 100 yuan per person; the afternoon tea is also very cost-effective, and the spring afternoon tea desserts and salty snacks are delicious. The spiral staircase and chandelier in the important lobby are so beautiful!

Unfortunately, the Chinese restaurant is being adjusted, but I booked a view seat at the Monet restaurant in advance! The purple a**osphere is so romantic, and I finally got to eat the traditional foie gras Wellington steak... I think there are still many foreign tourists who come here to eat and stay in the hotel.

The sun pool and gym are still well maintained! Life Fitness equipment is clean; the service of this hotel has always been online, the staff will take the initiative to greet the guests when they see them, the central air conditioning is very powerful, the environmentally friendly bottle of shower gel and shampoo is also very good, the guest rooms are cleaned every day, and I will stay in New World next time I come to Dalian.

If you want to experience the nightlife of Dalian with a few friends, this is definitely a good place. The grilled shellfish inside is very fresh and can taste sweet! Let's talk about the service of the hotel. This city of Dalian left a deep impression on me. First of all, the service industry has a very good attitude. I had breakfast at Yoshinoya, and the waiter said to me very apologetically that the beef patties were a little mushy. Including when I was at the New Century Hotel, the lobby manager would say good morning to me unexpectedly every morning, and when I checked out, the guy at the front desk didn't forget to say byebye with a smile. This kind of comfortable service attitude is something I haven't experienced in other cities. If you have to pick out the shortcomings of this hotel, it's that the windows are a little dirty, and there is no small soap in the bathroom. But I think compared with the overall smooth service speed and excellent service quality, this is nothing. I think if I have the chance, I will come to Dalian again, not only because of the vast sea, but also because of the comfortable Dalian people and the excellent service quality!

The actual situation is that the door is thick and heavy. When entering and leaving frequently in the morning and afternoon, the sound of closing the door causes strong tremors on the walls, doors and windows, and writing desk of the room. It is suggested that the hotel can install some cushioning materials on the door frames of the guest rooms to reduce the impact, noise and tremor, so that the more "nervous" hotel guests can also get some restful sleep.
